<s> he rushed to the gate <\s>
<s> she was walking swiftly on the heels of the straggling children <\s>
<s> she turned her head he saw her hand make a little flitting gesture then she sped on and the trailing family blotted her out from his view <\s>
<s> the words of a comic song paddington groan worst ever known he gave a sepulchral paddington groan came into his head and he sped incontinently back to reading station <\s>
<s> all the way up to london and down to wansdon he sat with the heart of the trail open on his knee knitting in his head a poem so full of feeling that it would not rhyme <\s>
<s> xii caprice fleur sped on <\s>
<s> she had need of rapid motion she was late and wanted all her wits about her when she got in <\s>
<s> she passed the islands the station and hotel and was about to take the ferry when she saw a skiff with a young man standing up in it and holding to the bushes <\s>
<s> miss forsyte he said let me put you across <\s>
<s> i've come on purpose <\s>
<s> she looked at him in blank amazement <\s>
<s> it's all right i've been having tea with your people <\s>
<s> i thought i'd save you the last bit <\s>
<s> it's on my way i'm just off back to pangbourne <\s>
<s> i saw you at the picture gallery you remember when your father invited me to see his pictures <\s>
<s> said fleur yes the handkerchief <\s>
<s> to this young man she owed jon and taking his hand she stepped down into the skiff <\s>
<s> still emotional and a little out of breath she sat silent not so the young man <\s>
<s> she had never heard any one say so much in so short a time <\s>
<s> he told her his age twenty four his weight ten stone eleven his place of residence not far away described his sensations under fire and what it felt like to be gassed criticized the juno mentioned his own conception of that goddess commented on the goya copy said fleur was not too awfully like it sketched in rapidly the condition of england spoke of monsieur profond or whatever his name was as an awful sport thought her father had some ripping pictures and some rather dug up hoped he might row down again and take her on the river because he was quite trustworthy inquired her opinion of tchekov gave her his own wished they could go to the russian ballet together some time considered the name fleur forsyte simply topping cursed his people for giving him the name of michael on the top of mont outlined his father and said that if she wanted a good book she should read job his father was rather like job while job still had land <\s>
<s> but job didn't have land fleur murmured he only had flocks and herds and moved on <\s>
<s> answered michael mont i wish my gov'nor would move on <\s>
<s> not that i want his land <\s>
<s> land's an awful bore in these days don't you think <\s>
<s> we never have it in my family said fleur <\s>
<s> we have everything else <\s>
<s> i believe one of my great uncles once had a sentimental farm in dorset because we came from there originally but it cost him more than it made him happy <\s>
<s> did he sell it <\s>
<s> no he kept it <\s>
<s> because nobody would buy it <\s>
<s> good for the old boy <\s>
<s> no it wasn't good for him <\s>
<s> father says it soured him <\s>
<s> his name was swithin <\s>
<s> what a corking name <\s>
<s> do you know that we're getting farther off not nearer <\s>
<s> cried mont dipping his sculls vaguely it's good to meet a girl who's got wit <\s>
<s> but better to meet a young man who's got it in the plural <\s>
<s> young mont raised a hand to tear his hair <\s>
<s> it's thick enough to bear a scratch <\s>
<s> do you mind sculling <\s>
<s> i want to get in <\s>
<s> said mont but when you get in you see i shan't see you any more to day <\s>
<s> fini as the french girl said when she jumped on her bed after saying her prayers <\s>
<s> don't you bless the day that gave you a french mother and a name like yours <\s>
<s> i like my name but father gave it me <\s>
<s> mother wanted me called marguerite <\s>
<s> do you mind calling me m <\s>

<s> it's in the spirit of the age <\s>
<s> i don't mind anything so long as i get in <\s>
<s> mont caught a little crab and answered that was a nasty one <\s>
<s> and he did for several strokes looking at her with rueful eagerness <\s>

<s> if you don't row i shall get out and swim <\s>
<s> then i could come in after you <\s>
<s> mont i'm late and tired please put me on shore at once <\s>
<s> when she stepped out on to the garden landing stage he rose and grasping his hair with both hands looked at her <\s>
<s> cried the irrepressible mont <\s>
<s> i know you're going to say out damned hair fleur whisked round threw him a wave of her hand <\s>
<s> she called and was gone among the rose trees <\s>
<s> she looked at her wrist watch and the windows of the house <\s>
<s> it struck her as curiously uninhabited <\s>
<s> the pigeons were just gathering to roost and sunlight slanted on the dovecot on their snowy feathers and beyond in a shower on the top boughs of the woods <\s>
<s> the click of billiard balls came from the ingle nook jack cardigan no doubt a faint rustling too from an eucalyptus tree startling southerner in this old english garden <\s>
<s> she reached the verandah and was passing in but stopped at the sound of voices from the drawing room to her left <\s>
<s> from behind the verandah screen which fenced the ingle nook she heard these words i don't annette <\s>
<s> did father know that he called her mother annette <\s>
<s> always on the side of her father as children are ever on one side or the other in houses where relations are a little strained she stood uncertain <\s>
<s> her mother was speaking in her low pleasing slightly metallic voice one word she caught demain <\s>
<s> and profond's answer all right <\s>
<s> a little sound came out into the stillness <\s>
<s> then profond's voice i'm takin a small stroll <\s>
<s> fleur darted through the window into the morning room <\s>
<s> there he came from the drawing room crossing the verandah down the lawn and the click of billiard balls which in listening for other sounds she had ceased to hear began again <\s>
<s> she shook herself passed into the hall and opened the drawing room door <\s>
<s> her mother was sitting on the sofa between the windows her knees crossed her head resting on a cushion her lips half parted her eyes half closed <\s>
<s> she looked extraordinarily handsome <\s>
<s> here you are fleur <\s>
<s> your father is beginning to fuss <\s>

<s> i go up to london with your aunt <\s>

<s> they're all going back i suppose <\s>
<s> yes all you will console your father <\s>
<s> fleur crossed the room stooped received a kiss on her forehead and went out past the impress of a form on the sofa cushions in the other corner <\s>
<s> fleur was by no means the old fashioned daughter who demands the regulation of her parents lives in accordance with the standard imposed upon herself <\s>
<s> she claimed to regulate her own life not those of others besides an unerring instinct for what was likely to advantage her own case was already at work <\s>
<s> in a disturbed domestic atmosphere the heart she had set on jon would have a better chance <\s>

<s> he told her his age twenty four his weight ten stone eleven his place of residence not far away described his sensations under fire and what it felt like to be gassed criticized the juno mentioned his own conception of that goddess commented on the goya copy said fleur was not too awfully like it sketched in rapidly the condition of england spoke of monsieur profond or whatever his name was as an awful sport thought her father had some ripping pictures and some rather dug up hoped he might row down again and take her on the river because he was quite trustworthy inquired her opinion of tchekov gave her his own wished they could go to the russian ballet together some time considered the name fleur forsyte simply topping cursed his people for giving him the name of michael on the top of mont outlined his father and said that if she wanted a good book she should read job his father was rather like job while job still had land <\s>
<s> but job didn't have land fleur murmured he only had flocks and herds and moved on <\s>
<s> answered michael mont i wish my gov'nor would move on <\s>
<s> not that i want his land <\s>
<s> land's an awful bore in these days don't you think <\s>
<s> we never have it in my family said fleur <\s>
<s> we have everything else <\s>
<s> i believe one of my great uncles once had a sentimental farm in dorset because we came from there originally but it cost him more than it made him happy <\s>
<s> did he sell it <\s>
<s> no he kept it <\s>
<s> because nobody would buy it <\s>
<s> good for the old boy <\s>
<s> no it wasn't good for him <\s>

<s> what a corking name <\s>

<s> but better to meet a young man who's got it in the plural <\s>

<s> it's thick enough to bear a scratch <\s>
<s> do you mind sculling <\s>

<s> it struck her as curiously uninhabited <\s>

<s> did father know that he called her mother annette <\s>

<s> fleur crossed the room stooped received a kiss on her forehead and went out past the impress of a form on the sofa cushions in the other corner <\s>
<s> fleur was by no means the old fashioned daughter who demands the regulation of her parents lives in accordance with the standard imposed upon herself <\s>
<s> she claimed to regulate her own life not those of others besides an unerring instinct for what was likely to advantage her own case was already at work <\s>

<s> she reached the verandah and was passing in but stopped at the sound of voices from the drawing room to her left <\s>

<s> did father know that he called her mother annette <\s>
<s> always on the side of her father as children are ever on one side or the other in houses where relations are a little strained she stood uncertain <\s>

<s> yes all you will console your father <\s>
<s> fleur crossed the room stooped received a kiss on her forehead and went out past the impress of a form on the sofa cushions in the other corner <\s>
<s> fleur was by no means the old fashioned daughter who demands the regulation of her parents lives in accordance with the standard imposed upon herself <\s>
<s> she claimed to regulate her own life not those of others besides an unerring instinct for what was likely to advantage her own case was already at work <\s>
<s> in a disturbed domestic atmosphere the heart she had set on jon would have a better chance <\s>

<s> what did her father know about jon <\s>
<s> she changed her dress so as to look as if she had been in some time and ran up to the gallery <\s>

<s> she was walking swiftly on the heels of the straggling children <\s>

<s> the words of a comic song paddington groan worst ever known he gave a sepulchral paddington groan came into his head and he sped incontinently back to reading station <\s>
<s> all the way up to london and down to wansdon he sat with the heart of the trail open on his knee knitting in his head a poem so full of feeling that it would not rhyme <\s>
<s> xii caprice fleur sped on <\s>
<s> she had need of rapid motion she was late and wanted all her wits about her when she got in <\s>

<s> said fleur yes the handkerchief <\s>
<s> to this young man she owed jon and taking his hand she stepped down into the skiff <\s>
<s> still emotional and a little out of breath she sat silent not so the young man <\s>
<s> she had never heard any one say so much in so short a time <\s>
<s> he told her his age twenty four his weight ten stone eleven his place of residence not far away described his sensations under fire and what it felt like to be gassed criticized the juno mentioned his own conception of that goddess commented on the goya copy said fleur was not too awfully like it sketched in rapidly the condition of england spoke of monsieur profond or whatever his name was as an awful sport thought her father had some ripping pictures and some rather dug up hoped he might row down again and take her on the river because he was quite trustworthy inquired her opinion of tchekov gave her his own wished they could go to the russian ballet together some time considered the name fleur forsyte simply topping cursed his people for giving him the name of michael on the top of mont outlined his father and said that if she wanted a good book she should read job his father was rather like job while job still had land <\s>
<s> but job didn't have land fleur murmured he only had flocks and herds and moved on <\s>
<s> answered michael mont i wish my gov'nor would move on <\s>
<s> not that i want his land <\s>

<s> she reached the verandah and was passing in but stopped at the sound of voices from the drawing room to her left <\s>
<s> from behind the verandah screen which fenced the ingle nook she heard these words i don't annette <\s>
<s> did father know that he called her mother annette <\s>
<s> always on the side of her father as children are ever on one side or the other in houses where relations are a little strained she stood uncertain <\s>
<s> her mother was speaking in her low pleasing slightly metallic voice one word she caught demain <\s>
<s> and profond's answer all right <\s>
<s> a little sound came out into the stillness <\s>
<s> then profond's voice i'm takin a small stroll <\s>
<s> fleur darted through the window into the morning room <\s>
<s> there he came from the drawing room crossing the verandah down the lawn and the click of billiard balls which in listening for other sounds she had ceased to hear began again <\s>
<s> she shook herself passed into the hall and opened the drawing room door <\s>
<s> her mother was sitting on the sofa between the windows her knees crossed her head resting on a cushion her lips half parted her eyes half closed <\s>
<s> she looked extraordinarily handsome <\s>
<s> here you are fleur <\s>
<s> your father is beginning to fuss <\s>
<s> what are you going to do to morrow mother <\s>
<s> i go up to london with your aunt <\s>
<s> i thought you might be <\s>
<s> will you get me a quite plain parasol <\s>
<s> they're all going back i suppose <\s>
<s> yes all you will console your father <\s>
<s> fleur crossed the room stooped received a kiss on her forehead and went out past the impress of a form on the sofa cushions in the other corner <\s>
<s> fleur was by no means the old fashioned daughter who demands the regulation of her parents lives in accordance with the standard imposed upon herself <\s>
<s> she claimed to regulate her own life not those of others besides an unerring instinct for what was likely to advantage her own case was already at work <\s>
<s> in a disturbed domestic atmosphere the heart she had set on jon would have a better chance <\s>
<s> none the less was she offended as a flower by a crisping wind <\s>
<s> if that man had really been kissing her mother it was serious and her father ought to know <\s>
<s> and her mother going up to town <\s>
<s> she turned into her bedroom and hung out of the window to cool her face which had suddenly grown very hot <\s>
<s> jon must be at the station by now <\s>
<s> what did her father know about jon <\s>
<s> she changed her dress so as to look as if she had been in some time and ran up to the gallery <\s>
<s> soames was standing stubbornly still before his alfred stevens the picture he loved best <\s>
<s> he did not turn at the sound of the door but she knew he had heard and she knew he was hurt <\s>
<s> she came up softly behind him put her arms round his neck and poked her face over his shoulder till her cheek lay against his <\s>
<s> he rushed to the gate <\s>
<s> she was walking swiftly on the heels of the straggling children <\s>
<s> she turned her head he saw her hand make a little flitting gesture then she sped on and the trailing family blotted her out from his view <\s>
<s> the words of a comic song paddington groan worst ever known he gave a sepulchral paddington groan came into his head and he sped incontinently back to reading station <\s>
<s> all the way up to london and down to wansdon he sat with the heart of the trail open on his knee knitting in his head a poem so full of feeling that it would not rhyme <\s>
<s> xii caprice fleur sped on <\s>
<s> she had need of rapid motion she was late and wanted all her wits about her when she got in <\s>
<s> she passed the islands the station and hotel and was about to take the ferry when she saw a skiff with a young man standing up in it and holding to the bushes <\s>
<s> miss forsyte he said let me put you across <\s>
<s> i've come on purpose <\s>
<s> she looked at him in blank amazement <\s>
<s> it's all right i've been having tea with your people <\s>
<s> i thought i'd save you the last bit <\s>
<s> it's on my way i'm just off back to pangbourne <\s>
<s> i saw you at the picture gallery you remember when your father invited me to see his pictures <\s>
<s> said fleur yes the handkerchief <\s>
<s> to this young man she owed jon and taking his hand she stepped down into the skiff <\s>
<s> still emotional and a little out of breath she sat silent not so the young man <\s>
<s> she had never heard any one say so much in so short a time <\s>
<s> he told her his age twenty four his weight ten stone eleven his place of residence not far away described his sensations under fire and what it felt like to be gassed criticized the juno mentioned his own conception of that goddess commented on the goya copy said fleur was not too awfully like it sketched in rapidly the condition of england spoke of monsieur profond or whatever his name was as an awful sport thought her father had some ripping pictures and some rather dug up hoped he might row down again and take her on the river because he was quite trustworthy inquired her opinion of tchekov gave her his own wished they could go to the russian ballet together some time considered the name fleur forsyte simply topping cursed his people for giving him the name of michael on the top of mont outlined his father and said that if she wanted a good book she should read job his father was rather like job while job still had land <\s>
<s> but job didn't have land fleur murmured he only had flocks and herds and moved on <\s>
<s> answered michael mont i wish my gov'nor would move on <\s>
<s> not that i want his land <\s>
<s> land's an awful bore in these days don't you think <\s>
<s> we never have it in my family said fleur <\s>
<s> we have everything else <\s>
<s> i believe one of my great uncles once had a sentimental farm in dorset because we came from there originally but it cost him more than it made him happy <\s>
<s> did he sell it <\s>
<s> no he kept it <\s>
<s> because nobody would buy it <\s>
<s> good for the old boy <\s>
<s> no it wasn't good for him <\s>
<s> father says it soured him <\s>
<s> his name was swithin <\s>
<s> what a corking name <\s>
<s> do you know that we're getting farther off not nearer <\s>
<s> cried mont dipping his sculls vaguely it's good to meet a girl who's got wit <\s>
<s> but better to meet a young man who's got it in the plural <\s>
<s> young mont raised a hand to tear his hair <\s>
<s> it's thick enough to bear a scratch <\s>
<s> do you mind sculling <\s>
<s> i want to get in <\s>
<s> said mont but when you get in you see i shan't see you any more to day <\s>

<s> fleur was by no means the old fashioned daughter who demands the regulation of her parents lives in accordance with the standard imposed upon herself <\s>
<s> she claimed to regulate her own life not those of others besides an unerring instinct for what was likely to advantage her own case was already at work <\s>

<s> she had need of rapid motion she was late and wanted all her wits about her when she got in <\s>

<s> still emotional and a little out of breath she sat silent not so the young man <\s>
<s> she had never heard any one say so much in so short a time <\s>
<s> he told her his age twenty four his weight ten stone eleven his place of residence not far away described his sensations under fire and what it felt like to be gassed criticized the juno mentioned his own conception of that goddess commented on the goya copy said fleur was not too awfully like it sketched in rapidly the condition of england spoke of monsieur profond or whatever his name was as an awful sport thought her father had some ripping pictures and some rather dug up hoped he might row down again and take her on the river because he was quite trustworthy inquired her opinion of tchekov gave her his own wished they could go to the russian ballet together some time considered the name fleur forsyte simply topping cursed his people for giving him the name of michael on the top of mont outlined his father and said that if she wanted a good book she should read job his father was rather like job while job still had land <\s>
<s> but job didn't have land fleur murmured he only had flocks and herds and moved on <\s>

<s> not that i want his land <\s>

<s> she passed the islands the station and hotel and was about to take the ferry when she saw a skiff with a young man standing up in it and holding to the bushes <\s>
<s> miss forsyte he said let me put you across <\s>
<s> i've come on purpose <\s>
<s> she looked at him in blank amazement <\s>
<s> it's all right i've been having tea with your people <\s>
<s> i thought i'd save you the last bit <\s>
<s> it's on my way i'm just off back to pangbourne <\s>
<s> i saw you at the picture gallery you remember when your father invited me to see his pictures <\s>
<s> said fleur yes the handkerchief <\s>
<s> to this young man she owed jon and taking his hand she stepped down into the skiff <\s>
<s> still emotional and a little out of breath she sat silent not so the young man <\s>
<s> she had never heard any one say so much in so short a time <\s>
<s> he told her his age twenty four his weight ten stone eleven his place of residence not far away described his sensations under fire and what it felt like to be gassed criticized the juno mentioned his own conception of that goddess commented on the goya copy said fleur was not too awfully like it sketched in rapidly the condition of england spoke of monsieur profond or whatever his name was as an awful sport thought her father had some ripping pictures and some rather dug up hoped he might row down again and take her on the river because he was quite trustworthy inquired her opinion of tchekov gave her his own wished they could go to the russian ballet together some time considered the name fleur forsyte simply topping cursed his people for giving him the name of michael on the top of mont outlined his father and said that if she wanted a good book she should read job his father was rather like job while job still had land <\s>
<s> but job didn't have land fleur murmured he only had flocks and herds and moved on <\s>
<s> answered michael mont i wish my gov'nor would move on <\s>
<s> not that i want his land <\s>
<s> land's an awful bore in these days don't you think <\s>
<s> we never have it in my family said fleur <\s>
<s> we have everything else <\s>
<s> i believe one of my great uncles once had a sentimental farm in dorset because we came from there originally but it cost him more than it made him happy <\s>
<s> did he sell it <\s>
<s> no he kept it <\s>
<s> because nobody would buy it <\s>
<s> good for the old boy <\s>
<s> no it wasn't good for him <\s>
<s> father says it soured him <\s>
<s> his name was swithin <\s>
<s> what a corking name <\s>
<s> do you know that we're getting farther off not nearer <\s>
<s> cried mont dipping his sculls vaguely it's good to meet a girl who's got wit <\s>
<s> but better to meet a young man who's got it in the plural <\s>
<s> young mont raised a hand to tear his hair <\s>
<s> it's thick enough to bear a scratch <\s>
<s> do you mind sculling <\s>
<s> i want to get in <\s>
<s> said mont but when you get in you see i shan't see you any more to day <\s>
<s> fini as the french girl said when she jumped on her bed after saying her prayers <\s>
<s> don't you bless the day that gave you a french mother and a name like yours <\s>
<s> i like my name but father gave it me <\s>
<s> mother wanted me called marguerite <\s>
<s> do you mind calling me m <\s>
<s> and letting me call you f <\s>
<s> it's in the spirit of the age <\s>
<s> i don't mind anything so long as i get in <\s>
<s> mont caught a little crab and answered that was a nasty one <\s>
<s> and he did for several strokes looking at her with rueful eagerness <\s>
<s> of course you know he ejaculated pausing that i came to see you not your father's pictures <\s>
<s> if you don't row i shall get out and swim <\s>
<s> then i could come in after you <\s>
<s> mont i'm late and tired please put me on shore at once <\s>
<s> when she stepped out on to the garden landing stage he rose and grasping his hair with both hands looked at her <\s>
<s> cried the irrepressible mont <\s>
<s> i know you're going to say out damned hair fleur whisked round threw him a wave of her hand <\s>
<s> she called and was gone among the rose trees <\s>
<s> she looked at her wrist watch and the windows of the house <\s>
<s> it struck her as curiously uninhabited <\s>
<s> the pigeons were just gathering to roost and sunlight slanted on the dovecot on their snowy feathers and beyond in a shower on the top boughs of the woods <\s>
<s> the click of billiard balls came from the ingle nook jack cardigan no doubt a faint rustling too from an eucalyptus tree startling southerner in this old english garden <\s>
<s> she reached the verandah and was passing in but stopped at the sound of voices from the drawing room to her left <\s>
<s> from behind the verandah screen which fenced the ingle nook she heard these words i don't annette <\s>
<s> did father know that he called her mother annette <\s>
<s> always on the side of her father as children are ever on one side or the other in houses where relations are a little strained she stood uncertain <\s>
<s> her mother was speaking in her low pleasing slightly metallic voice one word she caught demain <\s>
<s> and profond's answer all right <\s>
<s> a little sound came out into the stillness <\s>
<s> then profond's voice i'm takin a small stroll <\s>
<s> fleur darted through the window into the morning room <\s>
<s> there he came from the drawing room crossing the verandah down the lawn and the click of billiard balls which in listening for other sounds she had ceased to hear began again <\s>
<s> she shook herself passed into the hall and opened the drawing room door <\s>
<s> her mother was sitting on the sofa between the windows her knees crossed her head resting on a cushion her lips half parted her eyes half closed <\s>
<s> she looked extraordinarily handsome <\s>
<s> here you are fleur <\s>
<s> your father is beginning to fuss <\s>
<s> what are you going to do to morrow mother <\s>
<s> i go up to london with your aunt <\s>
<s> i thought you might be <\s>
<s> will you get me a quite plain parasol <\s>
<s> they're all going back i suppose <\s>
<s> yes all you will console your father <\s>
<s> fleur crossed the room stooped received a kiss on her forehead and went out past the impress of a form on the sofa cushions in the other corner <\s>
<s> fleur was by no means the old fashioned daughter who demands the regulation of her parents lives in accordance with the standard imposed upon herself <\s>
<s> she claimed to regulate her own life not those of others besides an unerring instinct for what was likely to advantage her own case was already at work <\s>
<s> in a disturbed domestic atmosphere the heart she had set on jon would have a better chance <\s>
<s> none the less was she offended as a flower by a crisping wind <\s>
<s> if that man had really been kissing her mother it was serious and her father ought to know <\s>
<s> and her mother going up to town <\s>
<s> she turned into her bedroom and hung out of the window to cool her face which had suddenly grown very hot <\s>
<s> jon must be at the station by now <\s>
<s> what did her father know about jon <\s>
<s> she changed her dress so as to look as if she had been in some time and ran up to the gallery <\s>
<s> soames was standing stubbornly still before his alfred stevens the picture he loved best <\s>
<s> he did not turn at the sound of the door but she knew he had heard and she knew he was hurt <\s>
<s> she came up softly behind him put her arms round his neck and poked her face over his shoulder till her cheek lay against his <\s>
<s> he rushed to the gate <\s>
<s> she was walking swiftly on the heels of the straggling children <\s>
<s> she turned her head he saw her hand make a little flitting gesture then she sped on and the trailing family blotted her out from his view <\s>
<s> the words of a comic song paddington groan worst ever known he gave a sepulchral paddington groan came into his head and he sped incontinently back to reading station <\s>
<s> all the way up to london and down to wansdon he sat with the heart of the trail open on his knee knitting in his head a poem so full of feeling that it would not rhyme <\s>

<s> did father know that he called her mother annette <\s>

<s> fleur crossed the room stooped received a kiss on her forehead and went out past the impress of a form on the sofa cushions in the other corner <\s>
<s> fleur was by no means the old fashioned daughter who demands the regulation of her parents lives in accordance with the standard imposed upon herself <\s>
<s> she claimed to regulate her own life not those of others besides an unerring instinct for what was likely to advantage her own case was already at work <\s>

<s> fleur was by no means the old fashioned daughter who demands the regulation of her parents lives in accordance with the standard imposed upon herself <\s>
<s> she claimed to regulate her own life not those of others besides an unerring instinct for what was likely to advantage her own case was already at work <\s>

<s> she had never heard any one say so much in so short a time <\s>
<s> he told her his age twenty four his weight ten stone eleven his place of residence not far away described his sensations under fire and what it felt like to be gassed criticized the juno mentioned his own conception of that goddess commented on the goya copy said fleur was not too awfully like it sketched in rapidly the condition of england spoke of monsieur profond or whatever his name was as an awful sport thought her father had some ripping pictures and some rather dug up hoped he might row down again and take her on the river because he was quite trustworthy inquired her opinion of tchekov gave her his own wished they could go to the russian ballet together some time considered the name fleur forsyte simply topping cursed his people for giving him the name of michael on the top of mont outlined his father and said that if she wanted a good book she should read job his father was rather like job while job still had land <\s>
<s> but job didn't have land fleur murmured he only had flocks and herds and moved on <\s>

<s> not that i want his land <\s>

<s> her mother was sitting on the sofa between the windows her knees crossed her head resting on a cushion her lips half parted her eyes half closed <\s>
<s> she looked extraordinarily handsome <\s>
<s> here you are fleur <\s>

<s> yes all you will console your father <\s>
<s> fleur crossed the room stooped received a kiss on her forehead and went out past the impress of a form on the sofa cushions in the other corner <\s>
<s> fleur was by no means the old fashioned daughter who demands the regulation of her parents lives in accordance with the standard imposed upon herself <\s>
<s> she claimed to regulate her own life not those of others besides an unerring instinct for what was likely to advantage her own case was already at work <\s>
<s> in a disturbed domestic atmosphere the heart she had set on jon would have a better chance <\s>
<s> none the less was she offended as a flower by a crisping wind <\s>
<s> if that man had really been kissing her mother it was serious and her father ought to know <\s>
<s> and her mother going up to town <\s>

<s> jon must be at the station by now <\s>
<s> what did her father know about jon <\s>
<s> she changed her dress so as to look as if she had been in some time and ran up to the gallery <\s>
<s> soames was standing stubbornly still before his alfred stevens the picture he loved best <\s>
<s> he did not turn at the sound of the door but she knew he had heard and she knew he was hurt <\s>
<s> she came up softly behind him put her arms round his neck and poked her face over his shoulder till her cheek lay against his <\s>
<s> he rushed to the gate <\s>
<s> she was walking swiftly on the heels of the straggling children <\s>
<s> she turned her head he saw her hand make a little flitting gesture then she sped on and the trailing family blotted her out from his view <\s>
<s> the words of a comic song paddington groan worst ever known he gave a sepulchral paddington groan came into his head and he sped incontinently back to reading station <\s>
<s> all the way up to london and down to wansdon he sat with the heart of the trail open on his knee knitting in his head a poem so full of feeling that it would not rhyme <\s>
<s> xii caprice fleur sped on <\s>
<s> she had need of rapid motion she was late and wanted all her wits about her when she got in <\s>
<s> she passed the islands the station and hotel and was about to take the ferry when she saw a skiff with a young man standing up in it and holding to the bushes <\s>
<s> miss forsyte he said let me put you across <\s>
<s> i've come on purpose <\s>
<s> she looked at him in blank amazement <\s>
<s> it's all right i've been having tea with your people <\s>
<s> i thought i'd save you the last bit <\s>
<s> it's on my way i'm just off back to pangbourne <\s>
<s> i saw you at the picture gallery you remember when your father invited me to see his pictures <\s>
<s> said fleur yes the handkerchief <\s>
<s> to this young man she owed jon and taking his hand she stepped down into the skiff <\s>
<s> still emotional and a little out of breath she sat silent not so the young man <\s>
<s> she had never heard any one say so much in so short a time <\s>
<s> he told her his age twenty four his weight ten stone eleven his place of residence not far away described his sensations under fire and what it felt like to be gassed criticized the juno mentioned his own conception of that goddess commented on the goya copy said fleur was not too awfully like it sketched in rapidly the condition of england spoke of monsieur profond or whatever his name was as an awful sport thought her father had some ripping pictures and some rather dug up hoped he might row down again and take her on the river because he was quite trustworthy inquired her opinion of tchekov gave her his own wished they could go to the russian ballet together some time considered the name fleur forsyte simply topping cursed his people for giving him the name of michael on the top of mont outlined his father and said that if she wanted a good book she should read job his father was rather like job while job still had land <\s>
<s> but job didn't have land fleur murmured he only had flocks and herds and moved on <\s>
<s> answered michael mont i wish my gov'nor would move on <\s>
<s> not that i want his land <\s>
<s> land's an awful bore in these days don't you think <\s>
<s> we never have it in my family said fleur <\s>
<s> we have everything else <\s>
<s> i believe one of my great uncles once had a sentimental farm in dorset because we came from there originally but it cost him more than it made him happy <\s>
<s> did he sell it <\s>
<s> no he kept it <\s>
<s> because nobody would buy it <\s>
<s> good for the old boy <\s>
<s> no it wasn't good for him <\s>

<s> what a corking name <\s>

<s> it's thick enough to bear a scratch <\s>
<s> do you mind sculling <\s>

<s> she came up softly behind him put her arms round his neck and poked her face over his shoulder till her cheek lay against his <\s>
<s> he rushed to the gate <\s>
<s> she was walking swiftly on the heels of the straggling children <\s>
<s> she turned her head he saw her hand make a little flitting gesture then she sped on and the trailing family blotted her out from his view <\s>
<s> the words of a comic song paddington groan worst ever known he gave a sepulchral paddington groan came into his head and he sped incontinently back to reading station <\s>
<s> all the way up to london and down to wansdon he sat with the heart of the trail open on his knee knitting in his head a poem so full of feeling that it would not rhyme <\s>
<s> xii caprice fleur sped on <\s>
<s> she had need of rapid motion she was late and wanted all her wits about her when she got in <\s>
<s> she passed the islands the station and hotel and was about to take the ferry when she saw a skiff with a young man standing up in it and holding to the bushes <\s>
<s> miss forsyte he said let me put you across <\s>
<s> i've come on purpose <\s>
<s> she looked at him in blank amazement <\s>
<s> it's all right i've been having tea with your people <\s>
<s> i thought i'd save you the last bit <\s>
<s> it's on my way i'm just off back to pangbourne <\s>
<s> i saw you at the picture gallery you remember when your father invited me to see his pictures <\s>
<s> said fleur yes the handkerchief <\s>
<s> to this young man she owed jon and taking his hand she stepped down into the skiff <\s>
<s> still emotional and a little out of breath she sat silent not so the young man <\s>
<s> she had never heard any one say so much in so short a time <\s>
<s> he told her his age twenty four his weight ten stone eleven his place of residence not far away described his sensations under fire and what it felt like to be gassed criticized the juno mentioned his own conception of that goddess commented on the goya copy said fleur was not too awfully like it sketched in rapidly the condition of england spoke of monsieur profond or whatever his name was as an awful sport thought her father had some ripping pictures and some rather dug up hoped he might row down again and take her on the river because he was quite trustworthy inquired her opinion of tchekov gave her his own wished they could go to the russian ballet together some time considered the name fleur forsyte simply topping cursed his people for giving him the name of michael on the top of mont outlined his father and said that if she wanted a good book she should read job his father was rather like job while job still had land <\s>
<s> but job didn't have land fleur murmured he only had flocks and herds and moved on <\s>
<s> answered michael mont i wish my gov'nor would move on <\s>
<s> not that i want his land <\s>
<s> land's an awful bore in these days don't you think <\s>
<s> we never have it in my family said fleur <\s>
<s> we have everything else <\s>
<s> i believe one of my great uncles once had a sentimental farm in dorset because we came from there originally but it cost him more than it made him happy <\s>
<s> did he sell it <\s>
<s> no he kept it <\s>
<s> because nobody would buy it <\s>
<s> good for the old boy <\s>
<s> no it wasn't good for him <\s>
<s> father says it soured him <\s>
<s> his name was swithin <\s>
<s> what a corking name <\s>
<s> do you know that we're getting farther off not nearer <\s>
<s> cried mont dipping his sculls vaguely it's good to meet a girl who's got wit <\s>
<s> but better to meet a young man who's got it in the plural <\s>
<s> young mont raised a hand to tear his hair <\s>
<s> it's thick enough to bear a scratch <\s>
<s> do you mind sculling <\s>
<s> i want to get in <\s>
<s> said mont but when you get in you see i shan't see you any more to day <\s>
<s> fini as the french girl said when she jumped on her bed after saying her prayers <\s>
<s> don't you bless the day that gave you a french mother and a name like yours <\s>
<s> i like my name but father gave it me <\s>
<s> mother wanted me called marguerite <\s>
<s> do you mind calling me m <\s>
<s> and letting me call you f <\s>
<s> it's in the spirit of the age <\s>
<s> i don't mind anything so long as i get in <\s>
<s> mont caught a little crab and answered that was a nasty one <\s>
<s> and he did for several strokes looking at her with rueful eagerness <\s>

<s> if you don't row i shall get out and swim <\s>
<s> then i could come in after you <\s>
<s> mont i'm late and tired please put me on shore at once <\s>
<s> when she stepped out on to the garden landing stage he rose and grasping his hair with both hands looked at her <\s>
<s> cried the irrepressible mont <\s>
<s> i know you're going to say out damned hair fleur whisked round threw him a wave of her hand <\s>
<s> she called and was gone among the rose trees <\s>
<s> she looked at her wrist watch and the windows of the house <\s>
<s> it struck her as curiously uninhabited <\s>
<s> the pigeons were just gathering to roost and sunlight slanted on the dovecot on their snowy feathers and beyond in a shower on the top boughs of the woods <\s>
<s> the click of billiard balls came from the ingle nook jack cardigan no doubt a faint rustling too from an eucalyptus tree startling southerner in this old english garden <\s>
<s> she reached the verandah and was passing in but stopped at the sound of voices from the drawing room to her left <\s>
<s> from behind the verandah screen which fenced the ingle nook she heard these words i don't annette <\s>
<s> did father know that he called her mother annette <\s>
<s> always on the side of her father as children are ever on one side or the other in houses where relations are a little strained she stood uncertain <\s>
<s> her mother was speaking in her low pleasing slightly metallic voice one word she caught demain <\s>
<s> and profond's answer all right <\s>
<s> a little sound came out into the stillness <\s>
<s> then profond's voice i'm takin a small stroll <\s>
<s> fleur darted through the window into the morning room <\s>
<s> there he came from the drawing room crossing the verandah down the lawn and the click of billiard balls which in listening for other sounds she had ceased to hear began again <\s>
<s> she shook herself passed into the hall and opened the drawing room door <\s>

<s> she looked extraordinarily handsome <\s>
<s> here you are fleur <\s>

<s> yes all you will console your father <\s>
<s> fleur crossed the room stooped received a kiss on her forehead and went out past the impress of a form on the sofa cushions in the other corner <\s>
<s> fleur was by no means the old fashioned daughter who demands the regulation of her parents lives in accordance with the standard imposed upon herself <\s>
<s> she claimed to regulate her own life not those of others besides an unerring instinct for what was likely to advantage her own case was already at work <\s>

<s> he told her his age twenty four his weight ten stone eleven his place of residence not far away described his sensations under fire and what it felt like to be gassed criticized the juno mentioned his own conception of that goddess commented on the goya copy said fleur was not too awfully like it sketched in rapidly the condition of england spoke of monsieur profond or whatever his name was as an awful sport thought her father had some ripping pictures and some rather dug up hoped he might row down again and take her on the river because he was quite trustworthy inquired her opinion of tchekov gave her his own wished they could go to the russian ballet together some time considered the name fleur forsyte simply topping cursed his people for giving him the name of michael on the top of mont outlined his father and said that if she wanted a good book she should read job his father was rather like job while job still had land <\s>
<s> but job didn't have land fleur murmured he only had flocks and herds and moved on <\s>
<s> answered michael mont i wish my gov'nor would move on <\s>
<s> not that i want his land <\s>
<s> land's an awful bore in these days don't you think <\s>
<s> we never have it in my family said fleur <\s>
<s> we have everything else <\s>
<s> i believe one of my great uncles once had a sentimental farm in dorset because we came from there originally but it cost him more than it made him happy <\s>
<s> did he sell it <\s>
<s> no he kept it <\s>
<s> because nobody would buy it <\s>
<s> good for the old boy <\s>
<s> no it wasn't good for him <\s>

<s> what a corking name <\s>

<s> but better to meet a young man who's got it in the plural <\s>

<s> it's thick enough to bear a scratch <\s>
<s> do you mind sculling <\s>

<s> it struck her as curiously uninhabited <\s>

<s> did father know that he called her mother annette <\s>

<s> fleur crossed the room stooped received a kiss on her forehead and went out past the impress of a form on the sofa cushions in the other corner <\s>
<s> fleur was by no means the old fashioned daughter who demands the regulation of her parents lives in accordance with the standard imposed upon herself <\s>
<s> she claimed to regulate her own life not those of others besides an unerring instinct for what was likely to advantage her own case was already at work <\s>

<s> she reached the verandah and was passing in but stopped at the sound of voices from the drawing room to her left <\s>

<s> did father know that he called her mother annette <\s>
<s> always on the side of her father as children are ever on one side or the other in houses where relations are a little strained she stood uncertain <\s>

<s> yes all you will console your father <\s>
<s> fleur crossed the room stooped received a kiss on her forehead and went out past the impress of a form on the sofa cushions in the other corner <\s>
<s> fleur was by no means the old fashioned daughter who demands the regulation of her parents lives in accordance with the standard imposed upon herself <\s>
<s> she claimed to regulate her own life not those of others besides an unerring instinct for what was likely to advantage her own case was already at work <\s>
<s> in a disturbed domestic atmosphere the heart she had set on jon would have a better chance <\s>

<s> what did her father know about jon <\s>
<s> she changed her dress so as to look as if she had been in some time and ran up to the gallery <\s>

<s> she was walking swiftly on the heels of the straggling children <\s>

<s> the words of a comic song paddington groan worst ever known he gave a sepulchral paddington groan came into his head and he sped incontinently back to reading station <\s>
<s> all the way up to london and down to wansdon he sat with the heart of the trail open on his knee knitting in his head a poem so full of feeling that it would not rhyme <\s>
<s> xii caprice fleur sped on <\s>
<s> she had need of rapid motion she was late and wanted all her wits about her when she got in <\s>

<s> said fleur yes the handkerchief <\s>
<s> to this young man she owed jon and taking his hand she stepped down into the skiff <\s>
<s> still emotional and a little out of breath she sat silent not so the young man <\s>
<s> she had never heard any one say so much in so short a time <\s>
<s> he told her his age twenty four his weight ten stone eleven his place of residence not far away described his sensations under fire and what it felt like to be gassed criticized the juno mentioned his own conception of that goddess commented on the goya copy said fleur was not too awfully like it sketched in rapidly the condition of england spoke of monsieur profond or whatever his name was as an awful sport thought her father had some ripping pictures and some rather dug up hoped he might row down again and take her on the river because he was quite trustworthy inquired her opinion of tchekov gave her his own wished they could go to the russian ballet together some time considered the name fleur forsyte simply topping cursed his people for giving him the name of michael on the top of mont outlined his father and said that if she wanted a good book she should read job his father was rather like job while job still had land <\s>
<s> but job didn't have land fleur murmured he only had flocks and herds and moved on <\s>
<s> answered michael mont i wish my gov'nor would move on <\s>
<s> not that i want his land <\s>

<s> she reached the verandah and was passing in but stopped at the sound of voices from the drawing room to her left <\s>
<s> from behind the verandah screen which fenced the ingle nook she heard these words i don't annette <\s>
<s> did father know that he called her mother annette <\s>
<s> always on the side of her father as children are ever on one side or the other in houses where relations are a little strained she stood uncertain <\s>
<s> her mother was speaking in her low pleasing slightly metallic voice one word she caught demain <\s>
<s> and profond's answer all right <\s>
<s> a little sound came out into the stillness <\s>
<s> then profond's voice i'm takin a small stroll <\s>
<s> fleur darted through the window into the morning room <\s>
<s> there he came from the drawing room crossing the verandah down the lawn and the click of billiard balls which in listening for other sounds she had ceased to hear began again <\s>
<s> she shook herself passed into the hall and opened the drawing room door <\s>
<s> her mother was sitting on the sofa between the windows her knees crossed her head resting on a cushion her lips half parted her eyes half closed <\s>
<s> she looked extraordinarily handsome <\s>
<s> here you are fleur <\s>
<s> your father is beginning to fuss <\s>
<s> what are you going to do to morrow mother <\s>
<s> i go up to london with your aunt <\s>
<s> i thought you might be <\s>
<s> will you get me a quite plain parasol <\s>
<s> they're all going back i suppose <\s>
<s> yes all you will console your father <\s>
<s> fleur crossed the room stooped received a kiss on her forehead and went out past the impress of a form on the sofa cushions in the other corner <\s>
<s> fleur was by no means the old fashioned daughter who demands the regulation of her parents lives in accordance with the standard imposed upon herself <\s>
<s> she claimed to regulate her own life not those of others besides an unerring instinct for what was likely to advantage her own case was already at work <\s>
<s> in a disturbed domestic atmosphere the heart she had set on jon would have a better chance <\s>
<s> none the less was she offended as a flower by a crisping wind <\s>
<s> if that man had really been kissing her mother it was serious and her father ought to know <\s>
<s> and her mother going up to town <\s>
<s> she turned into her bedroom and hung out of the window to cool her face which had suddenly grown very hot <\s>
<s> jon must be at the station by now <\s>
<s> what did her father know about jon <\s>
<s> she changed her dress so as to look as if she had been in some time and ran up to the gallery <\s>
<s> soames was standing stubbornly still before his alfred stevens the picture he loved best <\s>
<s> he did not turn at the sound of the door but she knew he had heard and she knew he was hurt <\s>
<s> she came up softly behind him put her arms round his neck and poked her face over his shoulder till her cheek lay against his <\s>
<s> he rushed to the gate <\s>
<s> she was walking swiftly on the heels of the straggling children <\s>
<s> she turned her head he saw her hand make a little flitting gesture then she sped on and the trailing family blotted her out from his view <\s>
<s> the words of a comic song paddington groan worst ever known he gave a sepulchral paddington groan came into his head and he sped incontinently back to reading station <\s>
<s> all the way up to london and down to wansdon he sat with the heart of the trail open on his knee knitting in his head a poem so full of feeling that it would not rhyme <\s>
<s> xii caprice fleur sped on <\s>
<s> she had need of rapid motion she was late and wanted all her wits about her when she got in <\s>
<s> she passed the islands the station and hotel and was about to take the ferry when she saw a skiff with a young man standing up in it and holding to the bushes <\s>
<s> miss forsyte he said let me put you across <\s>
<s> i've come on purpose <\s>
<s> she looked at him in blank amazement <\s>
<s> it's all right i've been having tea with your people <\s>
<s> i thought i'd save you the last bit <\s>
<s> it's on my way i'm just off back to pangbourne <\s>
<s> i saw you at the picture gallery you remember when your father invited me to see his pictures <\s>
<s> said fleur yes the handkerchief <\s>
<s> to this young man she owed jon and taking his hand she stepped down into the skiff <\s>
<s> still emotional and a little out of breath she sat silent not so the young man <\s>
<s> she had never heard any one say so much in so short a time <\s>
<s> he told her his age twenty four his weight ten stone eleven his place of residence not far away described his sensations under fire and what it felt like to be gassed criticized the juno mentioned his own conception of that goddess commented on the goya copy said fleur was not too awfully like it sketched in rapidly the condition of england spoke of monsieur profond or whatever his name was as an awful sport thought her father had some ripping pictures and some rather dug up hoped he might row down again and take her on the river because he was quite trustworthy inquired her opinion of tchekov gave her his own wished they could go to the russian ballet together some time considered the name fleur forsyte simply topping cursed his people for giving him the name of michael on the top of mont outlined his father and said that if she wanted a good book she should read job his father was rather like job while job still had land <\s>
<s> but job didn't have land fleur murmured he only had flocks and herds and moved on <\s>
<s> answered michael mont i wish my gov'nor would move on <\s>
<s> not that i want his land <\s>
<s> land's an awful bore in these days don't you think <\s>
<s> we never have it in my family said fleur <\s>
<s> we have everything else <\s>
<s> i believe one of my great uncles once had a sentimental farm in dorset because we came from there originally but it cost him more than it made him happy <\s>
<s> did he sell it <\s>
<s> no he kept it <\s>
<s> because nobody would buy it <\s>
<s> good for the old boy <\s>
<s> no it wasn't good for him <\s>
<s> father says it soured him <\s>
<s> his name was swithin <\s>
<s> what a corking name <\s>
<s> do you know that we're getting farther off not nearer <\s>
<s> cried mont dipping his sculls vaguely it's good to meet a girl who's got wit <\s>
<s> but better to meet a young man who's got it in the plural <\s>
<s> young mont raised a hand to tear his hair <\s>
<s> it's thick enough to bear a scratch <\s>
<s> do you mind sculling <\s>
<s> i want to get in <\s>
<s> said mont but when you get in you see i shan't see you any more to day <\s>

<s> fleur was by no means the old fashioned daughter who demands the regulation of her parents lives in accordance with the standard imposed upon herself <\s>
<s> she claimed to regulate her own life not those of others besides an unerring instinct for what was likely to advantage her own case was already at work <\s>

<s> she had need of rapid motion she was late and wanted all her wits about her when she got in <\s>

<s> still emotional and a little out of breath she sat silent not so the young man <\s>
<s> she had never heard any one say so much in so short a time <\s>
<s> he told her his age twenty four his weight ten stone eleven his place of residence not far away described his sensations under fire and what it felt like to be gassed criticized the juno mentioned his own conception of that goddess commented on the goya copy said fleur was not too awfully like it sketched in rapidly the condition of england spoke of monsieur profond or whatever his name was as an awful sport thought her father had some ripping pictures and some rather dug up hoped he might row down again and take her on the river because he was quite trustworthy inquired her opinion of tchekov gave her his own wished they could go to the russian ballet together some time considered the name fleur forsyte simply topping cursed his people for giving him the name of michael on the top of mont outlined his father and said that if she wanted a good book she should read job his father was rather like job while job still had land <\s>
<s> but job didn't have land fleur murmured he only had flocks and herds and moved on <\s>

<s> not that i want his land <\s>

<s> she passed the islands the station and hotel and was about to take the ferry when she saw a skiff with a young man standing up in it and holding to the bushes <\s>
<s> miss forsyte he said let me put you across <\s>
<s> i've come on purpose <\s>
<s> she looked at him in blank amazement <\s>
<s> it's all right i've been having tea with your people <\s>
<s> i thought i'd save you the last bit <\s>
<s> it's on my way i'm just off back to pangbourne <\s>
<s> i saw you at the picture gallery you remember when your father invited me to see his pictures <\s>
<s> said fleur yes the handkerchief <\s>
<s> to this young man she owed jon and taking his hand she stepped down into the skiff <\s>
<s> still emotional and a little out of breath she sat silent not so the young man <\s>
<s> she had never heard any one say so much in so short a time <\s>
<s> he told her his age twenty four his weight ten stone eleven his place of residence not far away described his sensations under fire and what it felt like to be gassed criticized the juno mentioned his own conception of that goddess commented on the goya copy said fleur was not too awfully like it sketched in rapidly the condition of england spoke of monsieur profond or whatever his name was as an awful sport thought her father had some ripping pictures and some rather dug up hoped he might row down again and take her on the river because he was quite trustworthy inquired her opinion of tchekov gave her his own wished they could go to the russian ballet together some time considered the name fleur forsyte simply topping cursed his people for giving him the name of michael on the top of mont outlined his father and said that if she wanted a good book she should read job his father was rather like job while job still had land <\s>
<s> but job didn't have land fleur murmured he only had flocks and herds and moved on <\s>
<s> answered michael mont i wish my gov'nor would move on <\s>
<s> not that i want his land <\s>
<s> land's an awful bore in these days don't you think <\s>
<s> we never have it in my family said fleur <\s>
<s> we have everything else <\s>
<s> i believe one of my great uncles once had a sentimental farm in dorset because we came from there originally but it cost him more than it made him happy <\s>
<s> did he sell it <\s>
<s> no he kept it <\s>
<s> because nobody would buy it <\s>
<s> good for the old boy <\s>
<s> no it wasn't good for him <\s>
<s> father says it soured him <\s>
<s> his name was swithin <\s>
<s> what a corking name <\s>
<s> do you know that we're getting farther off not nearer <\s>
<s> cried mont dipping his sculls vaguely it's good to meet a girl who's got wit <\s>
<s> but better to meet a young man who's got it in the plural <\s>
<s> young mont raised a hand to tear his hair <\s>
<s> it's thick enough to bear a scratch <\s>
<s> do you mind sculling <\s>
<s> i want to get in <\s>
<s> said mont but when you get in you see i shan't see you any more to day <\s>
<s> fini as the french girl said when she jumped on her bed after saying her prayers <\s>
<s> don't you bless the day that gave you a french mother and a name like yours <\s>
<s> i like my name but father gave it me <\s>
<s> mother wanted me called marguerite <\s>
<s> do you mind calling me m <\s>
<s> and letting me call you f <\s>
<s> it's in the spirit of the age <\s>
<s> i don't mind anything so long as i get in <\s>
<s> mont caught a little crab and answered that was a nasty one <\s>
<s> and he did for several strokes looking at her with rueful eagerness <\s>
<s> of course you know he ejaculated pausing that i came to see you not your father's pictures <\s>
<s> if you don't row i shall get out and swim <\s>
<s> then i could come in after you <\s>
<s> mont i'm late and tired please put me on shore at once <\s>
<s> when she stepped out on to the garden landing stage he rose and grasping his hair with both hands looked at her <\s>
<s> cried the irrepressible mont <\s>
<s> i know you're going to say out damned hair fleur whisked round threw him a wave of her hand <\s>
<s> she called and was gone among the rose trees <\s>
<s> she looked at her wrist watch and the windows of the house <\s>
<s> it struck her as curiously uninhabited <\s>
<s> the pigeons were just gathering to roost and sunlight slanted on the dovecot on their snowy feathers and beyond in a shower on the top boughs of the woods <\s>
<s> the click of billiard balls came from the ingle nook jack cardigan no doubt a faint rustling too from an eucalyptus tree startling southerner in this old english garden <\s>
<s> she reached the verandah and was passing in but stopped at the sound of voices from the drawing room to her left <\s>
<s> from behind the verandah screen which fenced the ingle nook she heard these words i don't annette <\s>
<s> did father know that he called her mother annette <\s>
<s> always on the side of her father as children are ever on one side or the other in houses where relations are a little strained she stood uncertain <\s>
<s> her mother was speaking in her low pleasing slightly metallic voice one word she caught demain <\s>
<s> and profond's answer all right <\s>
<s> a little sound came out into the stillness <\s>
<s> then profond's voice i'm takin a small stroll <\s>
<s> fleur darted through the window into the morning room <\s>
<s> there he came from the drawing room crossing the verandah down the lawn and the click of billiard balls which in listening for other sounds she had ceased to hear began again <\s>
<s> she shook herself passed into the hall and opened the drawing room door <\s>
<s> her mother was sitting on the sofa between the windows her knees crossed her head resting on a cushion her lips half parted her eyes half closed <\s>
<s> she looked extraordinarily handsome <\s>
<s> here you are fleur <\s>
<s> your father is beginning to fuss <\s>
<s> what are you going to do to morrow mother <\s>
<s> i go up to london with your aunt <\s>
<s> i thought you might be <\s>
<s> will you get me a quite plain parasol <\s>
<s> they're all going back i suppose <\s>
<s> yes all you will console your father <\s>
<s> fleur crossed the room stooped received a kiss on her forehead and went out past the impress of a form on the sofa cushions in the other corner <\s>
<s> fleur was by no means the old fashioned daughter who demands the regulation of her parents lives in accordance with the standard imposed upon herself <\s>
<s> she claimed to regulate her own life not those of others besides an unerring instinct for what was likely to advantage her own case was already at work <\s>
<s> in a disturbed domestic atmosphere the heart she had set on jon would have a better chance <\s>
<s> none the less was she offended as a flower by a crisping wind <\s>
<s> if that man had really been kissing her mother it was serious and her father ought to know <\s>
<s> and her mother going up to town <\s>
<s> she turned into her bedroom and hung out of the window to cool her face which had suddenly grown very hot <\s>
<s> jon must be at the station by now <\s>
<s> what did her father know about jon <\s>
<s> she changed her dress so as to look as if she had been in some time and ran up to the gallery <\s>
<s> soames was standing stubbornly still before his alfred stevens the picture he loved best <\s>
<s> he did not turn at the sound of the door but she knew he had heard and she knew he was hurt <\s>
<s> she came up softly behind him put her arms round his neck and poked her face over his shoulder till her cheek lay against his <\s>
<s> he rushed to the gate <\s>
<s> she was walking swiftly on the heels of the straggling children <\s>
<s> she turned her head he saw her hand make a little flitting gesture then she sped on and the trailing family blotted her out from his view <\s>
<s> the words of a comic song paddington groan worst ever known he gave a sepulchral paddington groan came into his head and he sped incontinently back to reading station <\s>
<s> all the way up to london and down to wansdon he sat with the heart of the trail open on his knee knitting in his head a poem so full of feeling that it would not rhyme <\s>

<s> fleur was by no means the old fashioned daughter who demands the regulation of her parents lives in accordance with the standard imposed upon herself <\s>
